<span class="content-bg rbottom" style=""><span class="r4" style="background: #999966"></span><span class="r3" style="background: #999966"></span><span class="r2" style="background: #999966"></span><span class="r1" style="background: #999966"></span></span></div>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&amp;nbsp;Star Wars: Episode I The Phantom Menace">"<i>Every saga has a beginning.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>―Tagline<span class="noprint"><sup><strong class="selflink">[src]</strong></sup></span></dd></dl></div>
</div></div></div></article></div></section></div></body></html>
<p><b><i>Star Wars</i>: Episode I <i>The Phantom Menace</i></b> is a <a href="/wiki/1999" title="1999">1999</a> <i><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars" title="Star Wars">Star Wars</a></i> film written and directed by <a href="/wiki/George_Lucas" title="George Lucas">George Lucas</a>. It was the fourth live-action film to be released in theaters, but is chronologically the first film of the saga. It was also the first and, to date, only <i>Star Wars</i> film to be re-released in 3D. The film was produced by <a href="/wiki/Rick_McCallum" title="Rick McCallum">Rick McCallum</a> and stars <a href="/wiki/Liam_Neeson" title="Liam Neeson">Liam Neeson</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ewan_McGregor" title="Ewan McGregor">Ewan McGregor</a>, <a href="/wiki/Natalie_Portman" title="Natalie Portman">Natalie Portman</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jake_Lloyd" title="Jake Lloyd">Jake Lloyd</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ian_McDiarmid" title="Ian McDiarmid">Ian McDiarmid</a> as the primary characters.
</p><p>The film takes place thirty-two years before <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope" title="Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope"><i>Star Wars</i>: Episode IV <i>A New Hope</i></a>, the first film released in the saga, and begins as two <a href="/wiki/Jedi/Canon" title="Jedi/Canon">Jedi</a> attempt to resolve a trade dispute and eventual <a href="/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo/Canon" title="Invasion of Naboo/Canon">invasion</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Planet/Canon" title="Planet/Canon">planet</a> <a href="/wiki/Naboo/Canon" title="Naboo/Canon">Naboo</a> by the <a href="/wiki/Trade_Federation/Canon" title="Trade Federation/Canon">Trade Federation</a>. Unknown to the Jedi is that the situation is being manipulated by <a href="/wiki/Darth_Sidious" title="Darth Sidious">Sheev Palpatine</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Senator/Canon" title="Senator/Canon">Senator</a> of Naboo and secretly a <a href="/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith/Canon" title="Dark Lord of the Sith/Canon">Dark Lord of the Sith</a> called Darth Sidious. The <a href="/wiki/Sith/Canon" title="Sith/Canon">Sith</a>, the ancient enemies of the Jedi, reveal themselves to the Jedi after a thousand <a href="/wiki/Year" title="Year">years</a> in hiding; while the Jedi discover a young <a href="/wiki/Tatooine/Canon" title="Tatooine/Canon">Tatooine</a> <a href="/wiki/Slavery/Canon" title="Slavery/Canon">slave</a> named <a href="/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker/Canon" title="Anakin Skywalker/Canon">Anakin Skywalker</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Chosen_One/Canon" title="Chosen One/Canon">Chosen One</a> destined to bring balance to <a href="/wiki/The_Force/Canon" title="The Force/Canon">the Force</a>—and who will grow up to become Darth Vader. Meanwhile, <a href="/wiki/Queen/Canon" title="Queen/Canon">Queen</a> <a href="/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala/Canon" title="Padmé Amidala/Canon">Padmé Amidala</a> of Naboo fights to save her people from the invasion.
</p><p><i>The Phantom Menace</i> was released in theaters on <a href="/wiki/May_19" title="May 19">May 19</a>, 1999, becoming the first <i>Star Wars</i> film since <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VI_Return_of_the_Jedi" title="Star Wars: Episode VI Return of the Jedi"><i>Star Wars</i>: Episode VI <i>Return of the Jedi</i></a> sixteen years earlier. The release was accompanied by extensive media coverage and great fan anticipation. Despite mixed reviews from critics and fans, the film grossed $924.3 million worldwide, making it the highest-grossing <i>Star Wars</i> film when unadjusted for inflation. The film was re-released on Blu-ray in <a href="/wiki/September" title="September">September</a> <a href="/wiki/2011" title="2011">2011</a>, and was re-released in theaters in 3D on <a href="/wiki/February_10" title="February 10">February 10</a>, <a href="/wiki/2012" title="2012">2012</a>. 
</p><p>The film was the first major story in the prequel era and began fifteen years of <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">canon</a> <i>Star Wars</i> storytelling that would primarily take place around the time of the prequel storyline. The success of the film allowed for the next two chapters of the prequel trilogy, as well as the <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars_(film)" title="Star Wars: The Clone Wars (film)"><i>Star Wars: The Clone Wars</i> film</a> and <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars_(TV_series)" title="Star Wars: The Clone Wars (TV series)">television series</a>. Numerous <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars_Legends" title="Star Wars Legends"><i>Star Wars</i> Legends</a> stories were also told in or influenced by <i>The Phantom Menace</i> and the prequels.
</p>

<th style="padding-top:0;"> Episode I<br/>THE PHANTOM MENACE

<td style="vertical-align:middle; font-size:90%; padding-bottom:0; color:black;"> <pre class="nostyle" style="overflow:hidden;">Turmoil has engulfed the
Galactic Republic. The taxation
of trade routes to outlying star
systems is in dispute.

Hoping to resolve the matter
with a blockade of deadly
battleships, the greedy Trade
Federation has stopped all
shipping to the small planet
of Naboo.

While the Congress of the
Republic endlessly debates
this alarming chain of events,
the Supreme Chancellor has
secretly dispatched two Jedi
Knights, the guardians of
peace and justice in the
galaxy, to settle the conflict....</pre>

</script><h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Synopsis">Synopsis</span><span class="editsection"><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace?action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit Synopsis section"><img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>Edit</a></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&amp;nbsp;Star Wars: Episode I The Phantom Menace">"<i>I have a bad feeling about this.</i>"<br/>"<i>I don't sense anything.</i>"<br/>"<i>It's not about the mission, Master. It's something…elsewhere…elusive.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>―Obi-Wan Kenobi to Qui-Gon Jinn<span class="noprint"><sup><strong class="selflink">[src]</strong></sup></span></dd></dl></div>

<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20111001152223/starwars/images/4/40/Dioxis.jpg"><img alt="Dioxis" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Dioxis.jpg" data-image-name="Dioxis.jpg" data-src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20111001152223/starwars/images/thumb/4/40/Dioxis.jpg/250px-Dioxis.jpg" height="106" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="250"><noscript><img alt="Dioxis" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Dioxis.jpg" data-image-name="Dioxis.jpg" height="106" src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20111001152223/starwars/images/thumb/4/40/Dioxis.jpg/250px-Dioxis.jpg" width="250"/></noscript></img></a> <figcaption> <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Dioxis.jpg"></a> <p class="caption">Qui-Gon and Obi-Wan prepare to fight their way out of the Trade Federation flagship.</p> </figcaption> </figure>
<p>There is trade dispute between the <a href="/wiki/Trade_Federation/Canon" title="Trade Federation/Canon">Trade Federation</a> and the outlying systems of the <a href="/wiki/Galactic_Republic/Canon" title="Galactic Republic/Canon">Galactic Republic</a>, which has led to a <a href="/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo/Canon" title="Invasion of Naboo/Canon">blockade</a> of the small <a href="/wiki/Planet/Canon" title="Planet/Canon">planet</a> of <a href="/wiki/Naboo/Canon" title="Naboo/Canon">Naboo</a>. <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor" title="Supreme Chancellor">Supreme Chancellor</a> <a href="/wiki/Finis_Valorum/Canon" title="Finis Valorum/Canon">Finis Valorum</a>, leader of the <a href="/wiki/Galactic_Senate/Canon" title="Galactic Senate/Canon">Galactic Senate</a>, has secretly dispatched two <a href="/wiki/Jedi/Canon" title="Jedi/Canon">Jedi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jedi_Master/Canon" title="Jedi Master/Canon">Master</a> <a href="/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn/Canon" title="Qui-Gon Jinn/Canon">Qui-Gon Jinn</a> and his <a href="/wiki/Padawan/Canon" title="Padawan/Canon">Padawan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi/Canon" title="Obi-Wan Kenobi/Canon">Obi-Wan Kenobi</a>, to serve as "ambassadors" to the Federation <a href="/wiki/Flagship/Canon" title="Flagship/Canon">flagship</a>, in order to meet with <a href="/wiki/Trade_Federation_Viceroy" title="Trade Federation Viceroy">Viceroy</a> <a href="/wiki/Nute_Gunray" title="Nute Gunray">Nute Gunray</a> and resolve the dispute. Unknown to them, the Trade Federation is in league with the mysterious <a href="/wiki/Darth_Sidious" title="Darth Sidious">Darth Sidious</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith/Canon" title="Dark Lord of the Sith/Canon">Dark Lord of the Sith</a>, who secretly orders Gunray to start this whole blockade and <a href="/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo/Canon" title="Invasion of Naboo/Canon">invade Naboo</a> (as well as implying that he would ensure that their invasion was made legal when asked if it was illegal by Gunray) and kill the two <a href="/wiki/Jedi/Canon" title="Jedi/Canon">Jedi</a> upon their arrival. Using poison gas, the Viceroy attempted to poison the two Jedi knights as an assassination attempt, but failed. After having to battle their way through squads of battle droids, Jinn and Kenobi make their way to the command deck where Gunray is located, but they are both locked out and forced to flee upon the arrival of two Destroyer Droids. Jinn and Kenobi's ship, <i><a href="/wiki/Radiant_VII/Canon" title="Radiant VII/Canon">Radiant VII</a></i>, is destroyed, and the two Jedi escape the assassination attempt by using <a href="/wiki/Force_speed" title="Force speed">knight speed</a> to get away from the destroyer droids and stow themselves aboard two separate <a href="/wiki/C-9979_landing_craft" title="C-9979 landing craft">Federation landing crafts</a> leaving for the surface of <a href="/wiki/Naboo" title="Naboo">Naboo</a> to begin the invasion. <a href="/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala" title="Padmé Amidala">Queen Amidala</a>, the queen of Naboo at the time, then contacts Gunray expressing her disapproval of their blockade of Naboo, with Gunray explaining that they wouldn't have done it without the approval of the senate. After threatening Gunray with the arrival of ambassadors sent by the Chancellor, Gunray claims that they have been greeted by no such ambassadors, leaving Amidala startled. Gunray, after ending communications with her, also tells his aide that they should disable all communications on the planet in case she suspected their invasion. Meanwhile, Amidala was conversing with Senator Palpatine regarding the recent attempt at negotiations and how Gunray claimed that they did not receive any ambassadors. Surprised, Palpatine he said that he had assurances from the Chancellor that his ambassadors did arrive. Senator Palpatine was not able to finish his sentence, however, because the hologram began to short out. Bibble suspected that the shorting out of communications was the first sign of an invasion from the Trade Federation.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130131223658/starwars/images/7/7b/TPM_Cast.png"><img alt="TPM Cast" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="TPM_Cast.png" data-image-name="TPM Cast.png" data-src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130131223658/starwars/images/thumb/7/7b/TPM_Cast.png/250px-TPM_Cast.png" height="106" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="250"><noscript><img alt="TPM Cast" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="TPM_Cast.png" data-image-name="TPM Cast.png" height="106" src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130131223658/starwars/images/thumb/7/7b/TPM_Cast.png/250px-TPM_Cast.png" width="250"/></noscript></img></a> <figcaption> <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:TPM_Cast.png"></a> <p class="caption">The Jedi liberate the Queen and her guards from the battle droid invasion.</p> </figcaption> </figure>
<p>On the planet's surface, Qui-Gon saves local native outcast <a href="/wiki/Jar_Jar_Binks/Canon" title="Jar Jar Binks/Canon">Jar Jar Binks</a> from being crushed by an <a href="/wiki/Multi-Troop_Transport" title="Multi-Troop Transport">MTT</a>. Later, <a href="/wiki/Single_Trooper_Aerial_Platform" title="Single Trooper Aerial Platform">STAPs</a> attack but are destroyed by Qui-Gon. Jar Jar Binks shows the two Jedi the way to an underwater <a href="/wiki/Gungan/Canon" title="Gungan/Canon">Gungan/Canon</a> settlement, <a href="/wiki/Otoh_Gunga" title="Otoh Gunga">Otoh Gunga</a>, escaping the Trade Federation army. Meanwhile, the <a href="/wiki/Trade_Federation" title="Trade Federation">Trade Federation</a> invades Naboo and captures their leader, <a href="/wiki/Queen/Canon" title="Queen/Canon">Queen</a> <a href="/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala/Canon" title="Padmé Amidala/Canon">Padmé Amidala</a>. The Jedi meet the Gungan leader, <a href="/wiki/Boss/Canon" title="Boss/Canon">Boss</a> <a href="/wiki/Nass" title="Nass">Nass</a>, and ask him to help the people of Naboo, but Nass refuses and sends them off in a <a href="/wiki/Tribubble_bongo" title="Tribubble bongo">bongo submarine</a>. They are attacked by an <a href="/wiki/Opee_sea_killer/Canon" title="Opee sea killer/Canon">opee sea killer/Canon</a> and a <a class="new" href="/wiki/Colo_claw_fish/Canon?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Colo claw fish/Canon (page does not exist)">colo claw fish</a> but both fish are eaten by a <a href="/wiki/Sando_aqua_monster" title="Sando aqua monster">sando aqua monster</a>. The Jedi, with Binks in tow, reach <a href="/wiki/Theed/Canon" title="Theed/Canon">Theed</a>, the capital city of Naboo, and rescue Queen Amidala from the <a href="/wiki/Trade_Defense_Force" title="Trade Defense Force">Trade Defense Force</a>. They depart for <a href="/wiki/Coruscant" title="Coruscant">Coruscant</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Galactic_Republic/Canon" title="Galactic Republic/Canon">Galactic Republic</a>'s capital planet, to ask for help from the Senate. An <a href="/wiki/Astromech_droid/Canon" title="Astromech droid/Canon">astromech droid</a> named <a href="/wiki/R2-D2" title="R2-D2">R2-D2</a> manages to repair the <a href="/wiki/J-type_327_Nubian_royal_starship" title="J-type 327 Nubian royal starship">Queen's starship</a> and they narrowly escape an attack from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Trade_Federation_battleship" title="Trade Federation battleship">Federation battleships</a>.
</p><p>Due to the damage the ship's <a href="/wiki/Hyperdrive/Canon" title="Hyperdrive/Canon">hyperdrive</a> sustained in the attack, the Queen's party is forced to land on the desert planet of <a href="/wiki/Tatooine/Canon" title="Tatooine/Canon">Tatooine</a> for repairs. While searching for a new hyperdrive generator, they befriend young <a href="/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker/Canon" title="Anakin Skywalker/Canon">Anakin Skywalker</a>, a slave boy, whose master is <a href="/wiki/Watto/Canon" title="Watto/Canon">Watto</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Toydarian/Canon" title="Toydarian/Canon">Toydarian</a> junk dealer.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130118131336/starwars/images/9/96/Anakin_Pod.png"><img alt="Anakin Pod" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Anakin_Pod.png" data-image-name="Anakin Pod.png" data-src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130118131336/starwars/images/thumb/9/96/Anakin_Pod.png/250px-Anakin_Pod.png" height="106" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="250"><noscript><img alt="Anakin Pod" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Anakin_Pod.png" data-image-name="Anakin Pod.png" height="106" src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130118131336/starwars/images/thumb/9/96/Anakin_Pod.png/250px-Anakin_Pod.png" width="250"/></noscript></img></a> <figcaption> <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Anakin_Pod.png"></a> <p class="caption">Anakin races ahead of Sebulba during the Boonta Eve Podrace.</p> </figcaption> </figure>
<p>Anakin is gifted with piloting and mechanical abilities, and has built an almost-complete droid named <a href="/wiki/C-3PO/Canon" title="C-3PO/Canon">C-3PO</a>. <a href="/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn/Canon" title="Qui-Gon Jinn/Canon">Qui-Gon Jinn</a> senses a strong presence of <a href="/wiki/The_Force/Canon" title="The Force/Canon">the Force</a> in Anakin, and feels that he may be the <a href="/wiki/Chosen_One/Canon" title="Chosen One/Canon">Chosen One</a> who will fulfill a prophecy by bringing balance to the Force. By entering Anakin into a <a href="/wiki/Podracing/Canon" title="Podracing/Canon">podrace</a>, Qui-Gon orchestrates a gamble in which the boy (alone, since Qui-Gon was unable to include the <a href="/wiki/Shmi_Skywalker_Lars/Canon" title="Shmi Skywalker Lars/Canon">youth's mother</a> in the bargain) will be released from slavery and they will win the parts needed for their ship. Anakin wins the race and joins the team as they head for <a href="/wiki/Coruscant/Canon" title="Coruscant/Canon">Coruscant</a>, where Qui-Gon plans to seek permission from the <a href="/wiki/Jedi_Council/Canon" title="Jedi Council/Canon">Jedi High Council</a> to train Anakin to be a Jedi. Meanwhile, <a href="/wiki/Darth_Sidious" title="Darth Sidious">Darth Sidious</a> sends his apprentice, <a href="/wiki/Darth_Maul/Canon" title="Darth Maul/Canon">Darth Maul</a>, to kill the two Jedi and capture the Queen. Maul appears just as the group is leaving the planet, and <a href="/wiki/Duel_on_Tatooine" title="Duel on Tatooine">duels</a> with Qui-Gon. The fight is cut short when Qui-Gon manages to escape his black-robed assailant by jumping onboard the Naboo Royal Starship as it takes off.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20111008200123/starwars/images/e/ef/Amidalabeforesenate.jpg"><img alt="Amidalabeforesenate" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Amidalabeforesenate.jpg" data-image-name="Amidalabeforesenate.jpg" data-src="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20111008200123/starwars/images/thumb/e/ef/Amidalabeforesenate.jpg/250px-Amidalabeforesenate.jpg" height="128" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="250"><noscript><img alt="Amidalabeforesenate" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Amidalabeforesenate.jpg" data-image-name="Amidalabeforesenate.jpg" height="128" src="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20111008200123/starwars/images/thumb/e/ef/Amidalabeforesenate.jpg/250px-Amidalabeforesenate.jpg" width="250"/></noscript></img></a> <figcaption> <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Amidalabeforesenate.jpg"></a> <p class="caption">Amidala and Palpatine plead before the Senate to intervene with Naboo's crisis.</p> </figcaption> </figure>
<p>On <a href="/wiki/Coruscant/Canon" title="Coruscant/Canon">Coruscant</a>, Qui-Gon informs the <a href="/wiki/Jedi_Council/Canon" title="Jedi Council/Canon">Jedi Council</a> of the mysterious attacker he encountered on <a href="/wiki/Tatooine/Canon" title="Tatooine/Canon">Tatooine/Canon</a>. Because of that being's obvious mastery of the Jedi arts, the Council becomes concerned that this development may indicate the reappearance of the <a href="/wiki/Sith/Canon" title="Sith/Canon">Sith</a>, a religious order who were followers of the <a href="/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force/Canon" title="Dark side of the Force/Canon">dark side of the force</a> and thought to be long gone. Qui-Gon also informs the Council about Anakin, hoping that he can be trained as a Jedi. After testing the boy and deliberating with one another, the Council refuses, deeming him too old for training according to the <a href="/wiki/Jedi_Code/Canon" title="Jedi Code/Canon">Jedi Code</a>. They are also concerned due to their sensing of a seemingly clouded future and a strong presence of fear in the boy. Meanwhile, <a href="/wiki/Senator/Canon" title="Senator/Canon">Senator</a> <a href="/wiki/Darth_Sidious" title="Darth Sidious">Sheev Palpatine</a> (of Naboo), warning of the corruption in the Senate, advises Queen Amidala to call for a <a href="/wiki/Vote_of_No_Confidence/Canon" title="Vote of No Confidence/Canon">Vote of No Confidence</a> in <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor/Canon" title="Supreme Chancellor/Canon">Supreme Chancellor</a> <a href="/wiki/Finis_Valorum/Canon" title="Finis Valorum/Canon">Finis Valorum</a>. Seeing no alternative, the Queen takes this advice when she addresses the Senate. Palpatine is among the candidates to replace the Supreme Chancellor, and the Queen later announces to Palpatine that she herself will return to their home planet to repel the invasion of her people. She is frustrated by the Senate's deliberation and lack of action, and feels that even if Palpatine is elected Chancellor, it will be too late. The Jedi Council sends the two Jedi to accompany the Queen back to <a href="/wiki/Naboo/Canon" title="Naboo/Canon">Naboo</a>, hoping to shed light on any Sith involvement.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130126035455/starwars/images/c/ca/Nass_on_Sacred_Place.png"><img alt="Nass on Sacred Place" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Nass_on_Sacred_Place.png" data-image-name="Nass on Sacred Place.png" data-src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130126035455/starwars/images/thumb/c/ca/Nass_on_Sacred_Place.png/250px-Nass_on_Sacred_Place.png" height="133" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="250"><noscript><img alt="Nass on Sacred Place" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Nass_on_Sacred_Place.png" data-image-name="Nass on Sacred Place.png" height="133" src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130126035455/starwars/images/thumb/c/ca/Nass_on_Sacred_Place.png/250px-Nass_on_Sacred_Place.png" width="250"/></noscript></img></a> <figcaption> <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Nass_on_Sacred_Place.png"></a> <p class="caption">Boss Nass at the Gungan Sacred Place.</p> </figcaption> </figure>
<p>Queen Amidala, back on Naboo, attempts to locate the Gungans at Otoh Gunga, but Jar-Jar, after searching Otoh Gunga, informs them that it was abandoned. He then led them to a sacred area which he was certain they were at. They then arrived at the Sacred Place, where the Gungans were waiting for them. After brief negotiations with Boss Nass, including Padme Naberrie revealing herself to be the true Queen Amidala, the Naboo formed an alliance with the <a href="/wiki/Gungan/Canon" title="Gungan/Canon">Gungan</a> people, uniting in battle against the <a href="/wiki/Trade_Federation/Canon" title="Trade Federation/Canon">Trade Federation</a>. Captain Panaka and several other security forces were also dispatched to rescue anyone imprisoned in the Trade Federation's prison camps, although they were only able to successfully extract a handful. Queen Amidala then gave their battle strategy: With the Grand Gungan Army acting as <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo/Canon" title="Battle of Naboo/Canon">a distraction</a> to the bulk of the main Trade Federation forces, the Naboo resistance led by Amidala, Obi-Wan, and Qui-Gon would infiltrate Theed via a secret entrance located inside one of the waterfalls. <a href="/wiki/Nute_Gunray/Canon" title="Nute Gunray/Canon">Nute Gunray</a>, taking the bait regarding the Gungan Army, informs Darth Sidious about the Grand Army, the latter then promptly ordering Gunray to wipe out the Gungans and the Naboo as the Trade Federation prepares for battle. <a href="/wiki/Captain/Canon" title="Captain/Canon">Captain</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tarpals" title="Tarpals">Tarpals</a> orders the <a href="/wiki/Gungan_Grand_Army/Canon" title="Gungan Grand Army/Canon">Gungan Grand Army</a> to start up their <a href="/wiki/Deflector_shield" title="Deflector shield">shield</a>, to protect them from ranged attack. <a href="/wiki/OOM-9" title="OOM-9">OOM-9</a> has his <a href="/wiki/Armored_Assault_Tank" title="Armored Assault Tank">tanks</a> fire first, but seeing them fail to penetrate the powerful shield, orders them to cease fire. <a href="/wiki/Daultay_Dofine" title="Daultay Dofine">Daultay Dofine</a> gives the command to activate the battle droids. These droids march through the shield, and its generator is destroyed. After much fighting against the Federation's droid army, defeat for the alliance seems imminent.
</p><p>However, victory comes when young Anakin Skywalker accidentally takes control of a <a href="/wiki/N-1_starfighter/Canon" title="N-1 starfighter/Canon">starfighter</a> and goes on to destroy the Federation's <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Trade_Federation_Battleship" title="Trade Federation Battleship">Droid Control Ship</a>, killing <a href="/wiki/Daultay_Dofine" title="Daultay Dofine">Daultay Dofine</a> and rendering the droid army useless. Meanwhile, Queen Amidala and her force fight their way back into the <a href="/wiki/Theed_Royal_Palace/Canon" title="Theed Royal Palace/Canon">royal palace</a> and capture <a href="/wiki/Nute_Gunray/Canon" title="Nute Gunray/Canon">Nute Gunray</a>.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20131206170906/starwars/images/0/08/DotF_TPM.png"><img alt="DotF TPM" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="DotF_TPM.png" data-image-name="DotF TPM.png" data-src="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20131206170906/starwars/images/thumb/0/08/DotF_TPM.png/250px-DotF_TPM.png" height="188" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="250"><noscript><img alt="DotF TPM" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="DotF_TPM.png" data-image-name="DotF TPM.png" height="188" src="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20131206170906/starwars/images/thumb/0/08/DotF_TPM.png/250px-DotF_TPM.png" width="250"/></noscript></img></a> <figcaption> <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:DotF_TPM.png"></a> <p class="caption">Qui-Gon and Obi-Wan fight against Darth Maul during the Battle of Naboo.</p> </figcaption> </figure>
<p>At the same time, in a Theed <a href="/wiki/Hangar" title="Hangar">hangar bay</a>, <a href="/wiki/Darth_Maul/Canon" title="Darth Maul/Canon">Darth Maul</a> (an apprentice of the Sith Lord Palpatine) has been engaging in combat with the two Jedi, using a <a href="/wiki/Double-bladed_lightsaber/Canon" title="Double-bladed lightsaber/Canon">double-bladed lightsaber</a>. The battle moves from the hangar, across a series of catwalks, to the <a href="/wiki/Plasma_Refinery_Complex" title="Plasma Refinery Complex">Theed Generator Complex</a>. During the fight, Obi-Wan is separated from his master when he is kicked off of a catwalk and falls. He grabs the edge of another catwalk below and jumps back up to where Qui-Gon and Maul continue to fight. By this time, Qui-Gon and Maul have become separated by a force field in the entrance to the Generator Room. Obi-Wan catches up to them, but is divided from his master by four force fields. When the force fields deactivates, Jinn and Maul continue their battle while Kenobi remains divided from the battle by one force field when they all reactivate. Maul suddenly hits Qui-Gon on the chin with his <a href="/wiki/Lightsaber/Canon" title="Lightsaber/Canon">lightsaber</a> handle, stunning him, then rams his lightsaber straight into Qui-Gon's chest, mortally wounding him. Heartbroken, Obi-Wan redoubles his assault upon Maul and chops Maul's lightsaber in half, but Maul almost kills Kenobi when he <a href="/wiki/Telekinesis#Force_Push" title="Telekinesis">Force pushes</a> him over the edge of a melting pit. Obi-Wan saves himself from falling when he manages to grab onto a pipe protruding from the wall of the pit. Maul then kicks the Jedi's lightsaber into the pit and prepares to finish him off. After Obi-Wan calms himself, he uses the Force to jump out of the pit and summons his fallen Master's lightsaber to his hand. Within an instant he lands behind the surprised Maul and cuts him in half; Maul's upper and lower body falls into the pit.
</p><p>Just before passing away, Qui-Gon instructs Obi-Wan to train Anakin to become a Jedi, reiterating that Anakin is the Chosen One. Obi-Wan gives his word that he will. The newly-elected Chancellor Palpatine arrives to congratulate Queen Amidala on her victory, as Nute Gunray is sent to stand trial for his crimes.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20111008202536/starwars/images/9/9a/Naboo_celebration.jpg"><img alt="Naboo celebration" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Naboo_celebration.jpg" data-image-name="Naboo celebration.jpg" data-src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20111008202536/starwars/images/thumb/9/9a/Naboo_celebration.jpg/250px-Naboo_celebration.jpg" height="106" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="250"><noscript><img alt="Naboo celebration" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Naboo_celebration.jpg" data-image-name="Naboo celebration.jpg" height="106" src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20111008202536/starwars/images/thumb/9/9a/Naboo_celebration.jpg/250px-Naboo_celebration.jpg" width="250"/></noscript></img></a> <figcaption> <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Naboo_celebration.jpg"></a> <p class="caption">The Gungans and the Naboo celebrate their victory.</p> </figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the battle, the Jedi Council names Obi-Wan a Jedi Knight. Kenobi conveys his Master's wish regarding Anakin Skywalker to <a href="/wiki/Yoda/Canon" title="Yoda/Canon">Yoda</a>, who reluctantly allows him to become Obi-Wan's apprentice. Qui-Gon's body is cremated, and <a href="/wiki/Mace_Windu" title="Mace Windu">Mace Windu</a> and Yoda agree that the Sith are definitely to blame for the tragedy. Being that there are <a href="/wiki/Rule_of_Two/Canon" title="Rule of Two/Canon">only ever two Sith at any given time</a> (a Master and an apprentice), both Masters believe that one must still remain.
</p><p>The Naboo and Gungans organize a great victory celebration on the streets of Theed, in front on the palace. Obi-Wan and Anakin are present, the younger now wearing formal <a href="/wiki/Jedi_apparel" title="Jedi apparel">Jedi attire</a>, and in his hair is a <a href="/wiki/Padawan_braid/Canon" title="Padawan braid/Canon">special braid</a>: the mark of a <a href="/wiki/Jedi/Canon" title="Jedi/Canon">Jedi</a> <a href="/wiki/Padawan/Canon" title="Padawan/Canon">Padawan</a>. Queen Amidala presents a gift of appreciation and friendship to Boss Nass and the Gungan people.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Development">Development</span><span class="editsection"><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit Development section"><img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>Edit</a></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Production">Production</span><span class="editsection"><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit Production section"><img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>Edit</a></span></h3>
<p>Along the lines of <i>The Young Indiana Jones Chronicles</i>, all three prequel films were originally intended to be written and shot as one large production, and released back-to-back.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[2]</a></sup>
</p><p>The budget of <i>Menace</i> was estimated US$115 million. Shooting took place from <a href="/wiki/June_26" title="June 26">June 26</a> to <a href="/wiki/September_30" title="September 30">September 30</a>, <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>. As with <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope" title="Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope"><i>Star Wars</i>: Episode IV <i>A New Hope</i></a>, Episode I's main exterior filming locations were in <a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisia</a>. The podrace was filmed in a canyon near <a href="/wiki/Sidi_Bouhlel" title="Sidi Bouhlel">Sidi Bouhlel</a> and <a href="/wiki/Oung_Jmel" title="Oung Jmel">Oung Jmel</a>. A set was built near Oung Jmel to represent <a href="/wiki/Mos_Espa" title="Mos Espa">Mos Espa</a> on Tatooine. The <a href="/wiki/Slave_Quarters_Row" title="Slave Quarters Row">Slave Quarters Row</a> were filmed in ksour's near <a href="/wiki/Tataouine" title="Tataouine">Tataouine</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ksar_Medenine" title="Ksar Medenine">Ksar Medenine</a>. Small parts were filmed in Royal <a href="/wiki/Caserta_Palace" title="Caserta Palace">Caserta Palace</a> in Italy, <a href="/wiki/Whippendell_Woods" title="Whippendell Woods">Whippendell Woods</a> and <a class="new" href="/wiki/Hever_Castle?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Hever Castle (page does not exist)">Hever Castle</a> in the <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_Kindom" title="wikipedia:United Kindom">United Kingdom</a>, but <i>Hever Castle</i> was later cut. Studio work was mainly done at <a href="/wiki/Leavesden_Studios" title="Leavesden Studios">Leavesden Studios</a> in the United Kingdom. More studio work is rumored to have taken place at <a class="new" href="/wiki/CTV_Services?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="CTV Services (page does not exist)">CTV Services</a> in <a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisia</a>.
</p><p>Unlike the latter two films in the series which were shot on <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/digital_video" title="wikipedia:digital video">digital video</a>, most of this film was shot in 35 mm, with a few scenes shot in digital video.
</p><p>This episode was also the first of the Saga to be referred to primarily by its number (<i>Episode One</i>) by media and fans, to contrast it with the <a href="/wiki/Original_trilogy" title="Original trilogy">classical saga</a> the public already knew. This reference also gave finally some sense to the riddling numbers IV-VI of the previous movies.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Release">Release</span><span class="editsection"><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit Release section"><img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>Edit</a></span></h3>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20111205190308/starwars/images/c/cf/EpIVaderShadowPoster-SWE.jpg"><img alt="EpIVaderShadowPoster-SWE" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="EpIVaderShadowPoster-SWE.jpg" data-image-name="EpIVaderShadowPoster-SWE.jpg" data-src="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20111205190308/starwars/images/thumb/c/cf/EpIVaderShadowPoster-SWE.jpg/200px-EpIVaderShadowPoster-SWE.jpg" height="296" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="200"><noscript><img alt="EpIVaderShadowPoster-SWE" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="EpIVaderShadowPoster-SWE.jpg" data-image-name="EpIVaderShadowPoster-SWE.jpg" height="296" src="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20111205190308/starwars/images/thumb/c/cf/EpIVaderShadowPoster-SWE.jpg/200px-EpIVaderShadowPoster-SWE.jpg" width="200"/></noscript></img></a> <figcaption> <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:EpIVaderShadowPoster-SWE.jpg"></a> <p class="caption">One of the most popular marketing posters for the film</p> </figcaption> </figure>
<p><i>The Phantom Menace</i> received enormous media-created hype, which made <a href="/wiki/Lucasfilm_Ltd." title="Lucasfilm Ltd.">Lucasfilm</a>'s $20 million advertising campaign – with the distinctive artwork of <i>Star Wars</i> series artist <a href="/wiki/Drew_Struzan" title="Drew Struzan">Drew Struzan</a> gracing the movie poster and other advertising – seem modest and almost unnecessary because of the unprecedented interest amongst both fans and the wider audience in the return of the franchise. Few film studios released films during the same week as the release of <i>The Phantom Menace</i>; among the more courageous were <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/DreamWorks" title="wikipedia:DreamWorks">DreamWorks</a> and <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Universal_Studios" title="wikipedia:Universal Studios">Universal Studios</a>, with the releases of <i><a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Love_Letter" title="wikipedia:The Love Letter">The Love Letter</a></i> and <i><a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Notting_Hill_(film)" title="wikipedia:Notting Hill (film)">Notting Hill</a></i> respectively. <i>The Love Letter</i> resulted in a box-office flop, whereas <i>Notting Hill</i> fared rather well and followed <i>The Phantom Menace</i> closely in second place.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[3]</a></sup> Challenger, Gray &amp; Christmas of Chicago, a work-issues consulting firm, estimated that 2.2 million full-time employees did not appear for work to attend the film, resulting in $293 million in lost productivity. <i><a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Wall_Street_Journal" title="wikipedia:The Wall Street Journal">The Wall Street Journal</a></i> reported that such a large number of workers announced plans to view premiere screenings that many companies shut down on the premiere day.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[4]</a></sup> Many fans began waiting outside cinema theaters as early as a month in advance of ticket sales.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[5]</a></sup>
</p><p>More theater lines appeared when it was announced that cinemas were not allowed to sell tickets in advance until two weeks into the release. This was done out of fear that family theater-goers would either be unable to receive tickets or would be forced to pay higher prices. Tickets were instead to be sold on a traditional first-come-first-serve basis.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[6]</a></sup> However, after meetings with the <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/National_Association_of_Theatre_Owners" title="wikipedia:National Association of Theatre Owners">National Association of Theatre Owners</a>, Lucasfilm agreed to allow advance ticket sales on <a href="/wiki/May_12" title="May 12">May 12</a>, <a href="/wiki/1999" title="1999">1999</a>, provided that there be a 12-ticket limit per customer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[7]</a></sup> As a result, however, some advance tickets were sold by "<a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ticket_resale" title="wikipedia:Ticket resale">scalpers</a>" as high as $100 apiece, which a distribution chief called "horrible", stating it was exactly what they wanted to avoid.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[8]</a></sup> <i><a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Variety_(magazine)" title="wikipedia:Variety (magazine)">Daily Variety</a></i> reported that theater owners received strict instructions from Lucasfilm that the film could only play in the cinema's largest auditorium for the first 8–12 weeks; no honor passes were allowed for the first eight weeks, and they were obligated to send their payments to distributor <a href="/wiki/Twentieth_Century_Fox_Film_Corporation" title="Twentieth Century Fox Film Corporation">20th Century Fox</a> within seven days.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[9]</a></sup>
Servers at the film's official website became gridlocked soon after the release of the first <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Teaser_trailer" title="wikipedia:Teaser trailer">teaser trailer</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[10]</a></sup> and many fans of the series paid full admission to see <i><a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Meet_Joe_Black" title="wikipedia:Meet Joe Black">Meet Joe Black</a></i> only to leave after the trailer had run. The same tradition followed months later when the <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Trailer_(film)" title="wikipedia:Trailer (film)">theatrical trailer</a> was featured in front of <i><a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wing_Commander_(film)" title="wikipedia:Wing Commander (film)">Wing Commander</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10">[11]</a></sup> The theatrical trailer caused even more notable media hype, because it not only premiered in theaters, but screened at the <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/National_Association_of_Theatre_Owners" title="wikipedia:National Association of Theatre Owners">ShoWest Convention</a> in <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Las_Vegas,_Nevada" title="wikipedia:Las Vegas, Nevada">Las Vegas</a>, and was aired on television on <i><a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Entertainment_Tonight" title="wikipedia:Entertainment Tonight">Entertainment Tonight</a></i> and <i><a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Access_Hollywood" title="wikipedia:Access Hollywood">Access Hollywood</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[12]</a></sup> An unusual marketing scheme was pursued across the <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="wikipedia:United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>, where the teaser trailer was released on <a href="/wiki/December_2" title="December 2">December 2</a>, <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a> and then pulled from theaters six weeks later.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[13]</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite worries about whether the film would be finished in time, two weeks prior to its debut Lucasfilm pushed the release date up from <a href="/wiki/May_21" title="May 21">May 21</a>, <a href="/wiki/1999" title="1999">1999</a> to <a href="/wiki/May_19" title="May 19">May 19</a>, <a href="/wiki/1999" title="1999">1999</a>. At the ShoWest Convention, Lucas stated that the change was to give the fans a "head start" by allowing them to view it over the week and allowing families the chance to view on the weekends. In a nod toward his future with digital technology, Lucas stated that the film would be released on four digital projectors on <a href="/wiki/June_18" title="June 18">June 18</a>, <a href="/wiki/1999" title="1999">1999</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[14]</a></sup> Eleven charity <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Premiere" title="wikipedia:Premiere">premieres</a> were staged across the United States on <a href="/wiki/May_16" title="May 16">May 16</a>, <a href="/wiki/1999" title="1999">1999</a>; receivings from the <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Los_Angeles,_California" title="wikipedia:Los Angeles, California">Los Angeles</a> event were given to the <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Elizabeth_Glaser_Pediatric_AIDS_Foundation" title="wikipedia:Elizabeth Glaser Pediatric AIDS Foundation">Elizabeth Glaser Pediatric AIDS Foundation</a> with corporate packages available for $5,000-$25,000.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[15]</a></sup> Other charity premieres included the <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dallas,_Texas" title="wikipedia:Dallas, Texas">Dallas</a> premiere for <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Children%27s_Medical_Center_(Dallas)" title="wikipedia:Children's Medical Center (Dallas)">Children's Medical Center</a>, the Aubrey Fund for Pediatric Cancer Research at the <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Memorial_Sloan-Kettering_Cancer_Center" title="wikipedia:Memorial Sloan-Kettering Cancer Center">Sloan-Kettering Hospital</a> in New York, the <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Big_Brothers_Big_Sisters_of_America" title="wikipedia:Big Brothers Big Sisters of America">Big Brother/Sister Assn.</a> of the <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Philadelphia,_Pennsylvania" title="wikipedia:Philadelphia, Pennsylvania">Philadelphia</a> premiere, and the <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Children%27s_National_Medical_Center" title="wikipedia:Children's National Medical Center">Children's National Medical Center</a> in <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Washington_D.C." title="wikipedia:Washington D.C.">Washington D.C.</a> A statement said that tickets were sold at $500 apiece and that certain sections were set aside for disadvantaged children.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[16]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Reception">Reception</span><span class="editsection"><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace?action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit Reception section"><img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>Edit</a></span></h2>
<p>Since it was the first <i>Star Wars</i> movie in 16 years, many <i>Star Wars</i> fans were excited when Episode I came out. After an enormous marketing campaign, with the distinctive artwork of <i>Star Wars</i> series artist <a href="/wiki/Drew_Struzan" title="Drew Struzan">Drew Struzan</a> gracing the movie poster and other advertising, there was almost unprecedented interest amongst both fans and the wider community in the return of one of the successful movie series. However, critical and fan reaction ranged from high praise to outright derision.
</p><p>The much-hyped special effects, while generally viewed as groundbreaking in their sheer scope, were perhaps less impressive than anticipated simply because of high expectations. This attitude was confirmed with the rival film, <i>The Matrix</i>, winning the visual effects Academy Award for that year over <i>The Phantom Menace</i>. It was the first time a <i>Star Wars</i> film lost in that Oscar competition category. Many critics heavily criticized the acting of <a href="/wiki/Natalie_Portman" title="Natalie Portman">Natalie Portman</a> and especially <a href="/wiki/Jake_Lloyd" title="Jake Lloyd">Jake Lloyd</a> as the young Anakin Skywalker. Some aspects of the scripting and direction were also criticized. Extra venom was directed at the character of <a href="/wiki/Jar_Jar_Binks" title="Jar Jar Binks">Jar Jar Binks</a>, who was regarded by some fans as purely a merchandising opportunity rather than a serious character in the film. Another source of dissatisfaction comes from the decision to explain Force-sensitivity with the introduction of <a href="/wiki/Midi-chlorian" title="Midi-chlorian">midi-chlorians</a>. Fan reaction was mixed too, with some fans praising the film while others having a negative opinion of it.
</p><p>However, despite some of the negative criticisms leveled at the film, many others gave praise to <i>The Phantom Menace</i>. William Arnold, of the Seattle Post-Intelligencer commented that the massive of hype of the film may have caused much of the negative reaction to the film, saying "it built expectations that can't possibly be matched and scuttled element of storytelling surprise". He also felt "it's well made and entertaining" and believed it was much better than similar box office fare released around that time period, such as <i>The Mummy</i> and <i>The Matrix</i> <a class="external autonumber exitstitial" href="http://seattlepi.nwsource.com/movies/starq.shtml" rel="nofollow">[1]</a>. David Cornelius of efilmcritic.com remarked that the better moments of the film "don't merely balance out the weaker ones- they topple them" <a class="external autonumber exitstitial" href="http://www.rottentomatoes.com/m/star_wars_episode_i_the_phantom_menace/" rel="nofollow">[2]</a>. Roger Ebert gave the film 3 and half out of four stars, calling it "an astonishing achievement in imaginative filmmaking," and stating that "Lucas tells a good story". Ebert comments that it was perfectly fine for the characters being a bit less compelling, seeing that they were just being introduced, and stating to "give me transparent underwater cities and vast hollow senatorial spheres any day." <a class="external autonumber exitstitial" href="http://rogerebert.suntimes.com/apps/pbcs.dll/article?AID=/19990517/REVIEWS/905170301/1023" rel="nofollow">[3]</a> Mark Dinning labels The Phantom Menace "A great work from a great director, and a blockbuster of quite the most swashbuckling kind". Many fans and critics also agree that the lightsaber duel between Qui-Gon, Obi-Wan, and Darth Maul—showcasing astounding choreography and <a href="/wiki/Ray_Park" title="Ray Park">Ray Park</a>'s martial arts skills—is a high point, and one of the best lightsaber duels in the entire <i>Star Wars</i> saga.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[17]</a></sup>
</p><p><i>Star Wars Episode I</i> was nominated for the <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Awards" title="wikipedia:Academy Awards">Academy Awards</a> on the categories of Best Visual Effects, Best Sound, and Best Sound Effects but it lost to <i><a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Matrix" title="wikipedia:The Matrix">The Matrix</a></i>. It won Best Motion Picture at the People's Choice Awards. It was also nominated for the <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saturn_Awards" title="wikipedia:Saturn Awards">Saturn Awards</a> on the categories of Best Science Fiction Film, Best Director (George Lucas), Best Actor (Liam Nesson), Best Supporting Actor (Ewan McGregor), Best Young Actor (Jake Lloyd), Best Young Actress (Natalie Portman), Best Supporting Actress (Pernilla August), Best Screenplay (George Lucas), Best Music (John Williams), Best Special Effects and Best Makeup, It won on the categories of Best Costume Design (Trisha Biggar) and Best Special Effects.<a class="external autonumber exitstitial" href="http://www.saturnawards.org/past.html" rel="nofollow">[4]</a>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="DVD_release">DVD release</span><span class="editsection"><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace?action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit DVD release section"><img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>Edit</a></span></h3>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20060501064051/starwars/images/1/1b/Ep1DVD.jpg"><img alt="Ep1DVD" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Ep1DVD.jpg" data-image-name="Ep1DVD.jpg" data-src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20060501064051/starwars/images/thumb/1/1b/Ep1DVD.jpg/200px-Ep1DVD.jpg" height="277" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="200"><noscript><img alt="Ep1DVD" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Ep1DVD.jpg" data-image-name="Ep1DVD.jpg" height="277" src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20060501064051/starwars/images/thumb/1/1b/Ep1DVD.jpg/200px-Ep1DVD.jpg" width="200"/></noscript></img></a> <figcaption> <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Ep1DVD.jpg"></a> <p class="caption"><i>The Phantom Menace</i> on <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars_DVD_releases" title="Star Wars DVD releases">DVD</a>.</p> </figcaption> </figure>
<p><i>Star Wars Episode I: The Phantom Menace</i> was released on <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars_DVD_releases" title="Star Wars DVD releases">DVD</a> in 2001; it was the first <i>Star Wars</i> film to be officially released on DVD. 
</p><p>The DVD features a commentary track by Lucas, producer Rick McCallum, editor <a href="/wiki/Ben_Burtt" title="Ben Burtt">Ben Burtt</a>, animation director <a href="/wiki/Rob_Coleman" title="Rob Coleman">Rob Coleman</a>, and visual effects supervisors <a href="/wiki/John_Knoll" title="John Knoll">John Knoll</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dennis_Muren" title="Dennis Muren">Dennis Muren</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Scott_Squires" title="Scott Squires">Scott Squires</a>. It includes seven deleted scenes completed specifically for the DVD, and <i>The Beginning: Making Episode I</i>, an hour-long documentary film drawn from more than 600 hours of footage, including an insider's look at Lucasfilm and ILM during the production. The viewer can access a multi-angle storyboard-to-animatic-to-film segment featuring the submarine and podrace lap 1 sequences. The DVD includes two documentary sources, five featurettes exploring the storyline, design, costumes, visual effects, and fight sequences in the film, and an award-winning twelve-part web documentary series chronicling the production. The <i>Duel of the Fates</i> music video featuring <a href="/wiki/John_Williams" title="John Williams">John Williams</a> was included on the DVD as well. The final special features included are a never-before-seen production photo gallery with a special caption feature, theatrical posters and print campaigns from around the world, a theatrical teaser and launch trailers, seven TV spots, <i>Star Wars: Starfighter - The Making of a Game</i> featurette from <a href="/wiki/LucasArts" title="LucasArts">LucasArts</a>, and a DVD-ROM weblink to exclusive <i>Star Wars</i> content.
</p><p>The DVD became the fastest selling DVD ever in the US, after 2.2 million copies were sold in its first week after release.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[18]</a></sup> However, some reviewers criticized the DVD for the excessive use of <a class="external text exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edge_enhancement">edge enhancement</a> that degraded the DVD's picture quality.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[19]</a></sup>
</p><p>At the DVD press conference for <i>Revenge of the Sith</i>, <i>Star Wars</i> prequel trilogy animation director, <a href="/wiki/Rob_Coleman" title="Rob Coleman">Rob Coleman</a> confirmed that the animation department at Lucasfilm has replaced the Yoda puppet from the original version of the film with a digital Yoda. This was done to better match up the look of the Yoda from <i>The Phantom Menace</i> with that of the other two films of the prequel trilogy, as well as with the Yoda from the original trilogy. This change has been, for the most part, welcomed by fans, in contrast to the original puppet Yoda as seen in <i>The Phantom Menace</i>.
</p><p>A preview of these changes can be viewed on the <i>Revenge of the Sith</i> DVD that was released on November 1st, 2005. The clip is included as part of "The Chosen One" featurette. When Coleman announced the change, he didn't, however, specify when the revised version of <i>The Phantom Menace</i> will be released. It is expected to be in an upcoming prequel trilogy box set, however.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19"><a href="#cite_note-19">[20]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Blu-ray_release">Blu-ray release</span><span class="editsection"><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace?action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit Blu-ray release section"><img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>Edit</a></span></h3>
<p><i>The Phantom Menace</i> was re-released along with Episodes II-VI on <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars_(Blu-ray)" title="Star Wars (Blu-ray)">Blu-ray</a> in <a href="/wiki/September" title="September">September</a> <a href="/wiki/2011" title="2011">2011</a>. <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20"><a href="#cite_note-20">[21]</a></sup>
For this release, the film went through a restoration process which restored the picture to its full frame (offering around 8% more picture when compared to its DVD release), increased the picture quality to be more clean and crisper while at the same time allowing <a href="/wiki/Industrial_Light_%26_Magic" title="Industrial Light &amp; Magic">ILM</a> to revisit and fix some visual effects and technical errors. The Blu-ray release was also marked by the replacement of the puppet for the CGI model of Yoda used in <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith" title="Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith"><i>Star Wars</i>: Episode III <i>Revenge of the Sith</i></a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="3D_release">3D release</span><span class="editsection"><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace?action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit 3D release section"><img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>Edit</a></span></h3>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130902214501/starwars/images/d/d1/Episode_I_3D_poster.png"><img alt="Episode I 3D poster" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Episode_I_3D_poster.png" data-image-name="Episode I 3D poster.png" data-src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130902214501/starwars/images/thumb/d/d1/Episode_I_3D_poster.png/180px-Episode_I_3D_poster.png" height="289" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"><noscript><img alt="Episode I 3D poster" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Episode_I_3D_poster.png" data-image-name="Episode I 3D poster.png" height="289" src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130902214501/starwars/images/thumb/d/d1/Episode_I_3D_poster.png/180px-Episode_I_3D_poster.png" width="180"/></noscript></img></a> <figcaption> <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Episode_I_3D_poster.png"></a> <p class="caption">Official poster for <i>The Phantom Menace</i> 3D release.</p> </figcaption> </figure>
<p>On <a href="/wiki/September_28" title="September 28">September 28</a>, <a href="/wiki/2010" title="2010">2010</a>, <a href="/wiki/StarWars.com" title="StarWars.com">StarWars.com</a> and Lucasfilm announced that the entire <i>Star Wars</i> saga would be converted to stereoscopic 3D and re-released in theaters and IMAX 3D, beginning with <i>Episode I</i>. <a href="/wiki/John_Knoll" title="John Knoll">John Knoll</a> and <a href="/wiki/Industrial_Light_%26_Magic" title="Industrial Light &amp; Magic">Industrial Light &amp; Magic</a> are supervising the conversion.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21"><a href="#cite_note-21">[22]</a></sup> The stereo conversion process has been in the works for several years, however, with George Lucas showing tests of the <i>Episode II</i> speeder chase scene and a reel from <i>Episode IV</i> in 3D during 2005's ShoWest in Las Vegas, and the speeder chase scene was demoed again by Texas Instruments as an emerging technology at SIGGRAPH 2007 in San Diego.
</p><p>Episode I's 3D release date, as announced by Lucasfilm on  <a href="/wiki/March_3" title="March 3">March 3</a>, <a href="/wiki/2011" title="2011">2011</a>, was <a href="/wiki/February_10" title="February 10">February 10</a>, <a href="/wiki/2012" title="2012">2012</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TFNTPMDate_22-0"><a href="#cite_note-TFNTPMDate-22">[23]</a></sup>
</p><p>On <a href="/wiki/January_28" title="January 28">January 28</a>, <a href="/wiki/2013" title="2013">2013</a>, Lucasfilm announced that the 3D releases of <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_II_Attack_of_the_Clones" title="Star Wars: Episode II Attack of the Clones"><i>Star Wars</i>: Episode II <i>Attack of the Clones</i></a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3DPostponed_23-0"><a href="#cite_note-3DPostponed-23">[24]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Deleted_scenes">Deleted scenes</span><span class="editsection"><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace?action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit Deleted scenes section"><img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>Edit</a></span></h3>
<ul><li><b>The Waterfall Sequence</b>—As Qui-Gon, Obi-Wan and Jar Jar arrive in the waterways of Theed, in the bongo, they surface just in front of a huge waterfall and have to vacate the vehicle in a hurry.
</li><li><b>Dawn Before the Podrace</b>—Anakin gets up early to prepare the pod for the race and has a brief chat with Padmé.
</li><li><b>Complete Podrace Grid Sequence</b>—This scene shows more of the participating racers and creatures in the crowd, later added on DVD.
</li><li><b>Extended Podrace Lap Two</b>—This lap shows some more of Sebulba's "creative interpretation of the rules" and further proof of just how special Anakin is, later added on DVD.
</li><li><b>Anakin's Scuffle With Greedo</b>—This was due to follow the podrace, to show Anakin's potential for aggression, but George Lucas cut it because he wanted Anakin to be shown as a genuinely good character who turns evil later in adulthood.
</li><li><b>Farewell to Jira</b>—This occurs as Qui-Gon and Anakin are leaving Mos Espa and Anakin stops briefly to say goodbye to Jira. One of Darth Maul's probe droids follows them for some time until Qui-Gon finally notices and destroys it before passing by the <i><a href="/wiki/Dusty_Duck" title="Dusty Duck">Dusty Duck</a></i>.
</li><li><b>The Air Taxi Sequence</b>—The taxi ride shows us about ten more seconds of Coruscant, later added on DVD.
</li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Soundtrack">Soundtrack</span><span class="editsection"><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace?action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit Soundtrack section"><img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>Edit</a></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint rellink"><img alt="Blue Glass Arrow" class="lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg" data-image-name="Blue Glass Arrow.svg" data-src="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20090726033133/starwars/images/thumb/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/20px-Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg.png" height="16" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="20"><noscript><img alt="Blue Glass Arrow" class="" data-image-key="Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg" data-image-name="Blue Glass Arrow.svg" height="16" src="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20090726033133/starwars/images/thumb/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/20px-Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg.png" width="20"/></noscript> Main article: <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars_Episode_I:_The_Phantom_Menace_(soundtrack)" title="Star Wars Episode I: The Phantom Menace (soundtrack)">Star Wars Episode I: The Phantom Menace (soundtrack)</a></img></div>
</dd></dl>
<p>Two separate soundtracks were released for <i>The Phantom Menace.</i> One, a traditional soundtrack, contained seventeen tracks selected from the movie. The second, an Ultimate Collector's Edition Soundtrack, compiled sixty-eight tracks of music, including several pieces that did not make it in to the final cut of the film.
</p><p>Major musical themes include:
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars_Main_Title" title="Star Wars Main Title">Star Wars Main Title</a>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Droid_Invasion_Theme" title="Droid Invasion Theme">Droid Invasion Theme</a>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Anakin%27s_Theme" title="Anakin's Theme">Anakin's Theme</a>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Duel_of_the_Fates" title="Duel of the Fates">Duel of the Fates</a>
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Novelization">Novelization</span><span class="editsection"><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace?action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit Novelization section"><img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>Edit</a></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint rellink"><img alt="Blue Glass Arrow" class="lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg" data-image-name="Blue Glass Arrow.svg" data-src="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20090726033133/starwars/images/thumb/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/20px-Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg.png" height="16" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="20"><noscript><img alt="Blue Glass Arrow" class="" data-image-key="Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg" data-image-name="Blue Glass Arrow.svg" height="16" src="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20090726033133/starwars/images/thumb/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/20px-Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg.png" width="20"/></noscript> Main article: <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars_Episode_I:_The_Phantom_Menace_(novel)" title="Star Wars Episode I: The Phantom Menace (novel)">Star Wars Episode I: The Phantom Menace (novel)</a></img></div>
</dd></dl>
<p>A <a href="/wiki/Novel" title="Novel">novelization</a> of the movie was written by <a href="/wiki/Terry_Brooks" title="Terry Brooks">Terry Brooks</a>. It includes three entire chapters of material created by Brooks and unique to the novel. The first two chapters of the book concern Anakin's next-to-last podrace and its aftermath, while a later chapter describes an encounter between Anakin and a wounded Tusken Raider in the desert.
</p><p>Brooks met with Lucas before writing the book and received his approval and guidance, including information about developments to come in Episodes II and III. This can be seen in such passages as the Tusken Raider scene, which ironically foreshadows the death of Anakin's mother in Episode II, and the passage leading up to Anakin's fight with the Rodian child <a href="/wiki/Greedo_the_Elder" title="Greedo the Elder">Greedo</a>, indicating that Anakin's anger derives from his anguish at Padmé's impending departure (foreshadowing the plot of Episode III).
</p><p>The novelization is especially well-known for a passage describing the history of the Sith, including <a href="/wiki/Darth_Bane" title="Darth Bane">Darth Bane</a>. According to Terry Brooks's memoir, <i>Sometimes the Magic Works</i>, Lucas spent an hour on the telephone with him discussing the history of the Jedi and the Sith. Therefore, the information on this subject provided in Brooks's novelization might derive from Lucas himself. The novelization is also the first mention of the <a href="/wiki/Stark_Hyperspace_War" title="Stark Hyperspace War">Stark Hyperspace War</a>.
</p><p>Brooks devotes an entire chapter of <i>Sometimes the Magic Works</i> to the writing of the Episode I novelization, which he claims to have been an extremely happy and fulfilling experience.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Continuity">Continuity</span><span class="editsection"><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace?action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit Continuity section"><img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>Edit</a></span></h2>
<p><i>The Phantom Menace</i> introduces the Senate Guards, who are garbed in blue armor similar to that of the Emperor's Royal Guard in <i>Return of the Jedi</i>. The Senate Guards are the predecessors to the Royal Guard. 
</p><p>During the credits at the end of the film, young <a href="/wiki/Anakin" title="Anakin">Anakin</a>'s theme is heard playing, but during the last moments of the film, this theme morphs into the first few notes of the <a href="/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker" title="Anakin Skywalker">Darth Vader</a> theme during the <a href="/wiki/The_Imperial_March" title="The Imperial March">Imperial March</a>, and, as the last logos of <a href="/wiki/THX" title="THX">THX</a> are scrolling by, three rasping breaths from Darth Vader's respirator can be heard, referencing Anakin's eventual change into Darth Vader.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Credits">Credits</span><span class="editsection"><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace?action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit Credits section"><img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>Edit</a></span></h2>

<ol class="references"><li id="cite_note-Leland_Chee_Date_Tweet-0"><a href="#cite_ref-Leland_Chee_Date_Tweet_0-0">↑</a> <span class="reference-text"><span class="plainlinks"><a class="image image-thumbnail link-external" href="https://twitter.com/HolocronKeeper/status/495972415458250752"><img alt="Twitter favicon" class="lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Twitter_favicon.png" data-image-name="Twitter favicon.png" data-src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20120608021255/starwars/images/thumb/3/36/Twitter_favicon.png/25px-Twitter_favicon.png" height="25" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="25"><noscript><img alt="Twitter favicon" class="" data-image-key="Twitter_favicon.png" data-image-name="Twitter favicon.png" height="25" src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20120608021255/starwars/images/thumb/3/36/Twitter_favicon.png/25px-Twitter_favicon.png" width="25"/></noscript></img></a> <a class="external text" href="https://twitter.com/HolocronKeeper/status/495972415458250752" rel="nofollow">@HolocronKeeper</a> (<a href="/wiki/Leland_Chee" title="Leland Chee">Leland Chee</a>) on <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Twitter" title="wikipedia:Twitter">Twitter</a></span>. “0 10 10-13 13 27 32 35 36” <small>(<a href="/wiki/File:Leland_Chee_Canon_Years.png" title="File:Leland Chee Canon Years.png">screenshot</a>)</small>—The tweet in question refers to the number of <a href="/wiki/In-universe" title="In-universe">in-universe</a> <a href="/wiki/Year" title="Year">years</a> between the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">canon</a> films and television shows. Using simple math, it can be deduced when <i>The Phantom Menace</i> takes place on the timeline.</span>
